#Articulo
<!-- START_3684f7162271b4651f47dc27b191c5d6 -->
## Articulo: Store
Método para la creación de una instancia de Articulo
params: [id_sucursal,nombre,foto,cantidad,stock_minimo,precio,descripcion,id_categoria,descuento_producto, cantidad_mayoreo, descuento_mayoreo, id_tipo_aplicacion_descuento_producto, id_tipo_aplicacion_descuento_mayoreo]
NOTA: id_tipo_aplicacion_descuento acepta los valores 1 y 2 (1: Precio, 2: Porcentaje)
NOTA 2: Al enviar descuento_mayoreo, se tiene que enviar cantidad_mayoreo

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/articulo/store" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/articulo/store",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`POST api/articulo/store`


<!-- END_3684f7162271b4651f47dc27b191c5d6 -->

<!-- START_4ea2b507a2157974e7feabdb14746077 -->

## Articulo: Por categoria
Método para mostrar una lista de Articulos por categoria
params: [id_categoria,page]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/articulo/por-categoria" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/articulo/por-categoria",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

> Example response:

```json
{
    "message": "Unauthenticated."
}
```

```javascript
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
```

### HTTP Request

<!-- START_3ec8d0da6df2ab07616255cdf8a1e513 -->
## Asistencia: Eliminar por sesión y Usuario
Devuelve la asistencia de un usuario y una sesión
params: [id_sesion, id_usuario, page]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/asistencia/eliminar-sesion-usuario" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/asistencia/eliminar-sesion-usuario",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

> Example response:

```json
{
```

### HTTP Request
`GET api/asistencia/eliminar-sesion-usuario`

`HEAD api/asistencia/eliminar-sesion-usuario`


<!-- END_3ec8d0da6df2ab07616255cdf8a1e513 -->

<!-- START_a55e2da55fa508fcc066fbe78b8e2df7 -->
## Asistencia: Destroy
Método para eliminar una instancia de Asistencia
params id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X DELETE "http://localhost/api/asistencia/destroy/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/asistencia/destroy/{id}",
    "method": "DELETE",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`DELETE api/asistencia/destroy/{id}`


<!-- END_a55e2da55fa508fcc066fbe78b8e2df7 -->

<!-- START_b358cf47a7ffa2efd89a0e49a0d22a53 -->
## Asistencia: Index
Método para mostrar una lista de Asistencia
params: [page]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/asistencia" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/asistencia",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

## Asistencia: Show
Método para mostrar una instancia de Asistencia
params: id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/asistencia/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/asistencia/{id}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

#Atleta
<!-- START_c1744b74297facfeca34d85bc47a4578 -->
## Atleta: Store
Método para la creación de una instancia de Atleta
params: [email,nombre,apellido_paterno,apellido_materno,telefono,fecha_nacimiento,sexo,tipo_sangre,consumer_token,id_titulo]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/atleta/store" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/atleta/store",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

`POST api/atleta/store`

## Atleta: Buscar
Método que hace la búsqueda de atletas por nombre, apellidos y email.

params: [q]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/atleta/buscar" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/atleta/buscar",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

### HTTP Request
`GET api/atleta/buscar`

`HEAD api/atleta/buscar`


<!-- END_c98ea467b27d508f2ab1f8b99938fce6 -->

<!-- START_e3dd8e10f45d097d9f031483d1980655 -->
## Atleta: Por sucursal Activos
Método que devuelve a los atletas de una sucursal que aún tengan visitas disponibles
en su membresía.

params: [id_sucursal]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/atleta/por-sucursal-activos" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/atleta/por-sucursal-activos",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

### HTTP Request
`GET api/atleta/por-sucursal-activos`

`HEAD api/atleta/por-sucursal-activos`

<!-- START_aabd76f9df137ef6ee978600ed1152b2 -->
## Atleta: Destroy
Método para eliminar una instancia de Atleta
params id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X DELETE "http://localhost/api/atleta/destroy/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/atleta/destroy/{id}",
    "method": "DELETE",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`DELETE api/atleta/destroy/{id}`


<!-- END_aabd76f9df137ef6ee978600ed1152b2 -->

## Atleta: Index
Método para mostrar una lista de Atleta
params: [page]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/atleta" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/atleta",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

### HTTP Request
`GET api/atleta`

`HEAD api/atleta`


<!-- END_e4ae20b472a13f41202a080fd00b4637 -->

<!-- START_7f3670869644787da2c96495f71cff67 -->
## Atleta: Show
Método para mostrar una instancia de Atleta
params: id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/atleta/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/atleta/{id}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

### HTTP Request

#Auth
<!-- START_a925a8d22b3615f12fca79456d286859 -->
## Auth: Login
Access the system through an email and a password.

Params: [email, password]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/auth/login" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/auth/login",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`POST api/auth/login`


<!-- END_a925a8d22b3615f12fca79456d286859 -->

#Clase
<!-- START_ed46d728a1aad48a0c3ddf36696cfe11 -->
## Clase: Store
Método para la creación de una instancia de Clase
El campo profesores debe mandarse como un arreglo con los ids de los usuarios que pueden impartir la clase.

Ejemplo: [1,4,5,2]
params: [id_sucursal,cupo,nombre,notas_especiales, profesores]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/clase/store" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/clase/store",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`POST api/clase/store`


<!-- END_ed46d728a1aad48a0c3ddf36696cfe11 -->

<!-- START_e08ed7e4b49c4846cd87752d38ac3474 -->
## Clase: Update
Método para la actualización de una instancia de Clase
El campo profesores debe mandarse como un arreglo con los ids de los usuarios que pueden impartir la clase.

Ejemplo: [1,4,5,2]
params: [id,id_sucursal,cupo,nombre,notas_especiales, profesores]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/clase/update" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/clase/update",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`POST api/clase/update`


<!-- END_e08ed7e4b49c4846cd87752d38ac3474 -->

<!-- START_7140902cfc23d95a579c32832b6071a7 -->
## Clase: Por sucursal y fecha
Método que devuelve las clases que tienen al menos una sesión en la fecha programada.

params: [id_sucursal, fecha]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/clase/por-sucursal-fecha" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/clase/por-sucursal-fecha",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

### HTTP Request

<!-- START_1de3a0e6d90c96824b3e9e7e0cc4fd31 -->
## Clase: Destroy
Método para eliminar una instancia de Clase
params id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X DELETE "http://localhost/api/clase/destroy/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/clase/destroy/{id}",
    "method": "DELETE",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`DELETE api/clase/destroy/{id}`


<!-- END_1de3a0e6d90c96824b3e9e7e0cc4fd31 -->

<!-- START_5ce05c3a80e7d7800d6f9eb94f34a82f -->
## Clase: Index
Método para mostrar una lista de Clase
params: [id_sucursal, q, page]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/clase" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/clase",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

### HTTP Request
`GET api/clase`

`HEAD api/clase`


<!-- END_5ce05c3a80e7d7800d6f9eb94f34a82f -->

<!-- START_5181fd34d49977c2fc5bc31a5b52eafb -->
## Clase: Show
Método para mostrar una instancia de Clase
params: id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/clase/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/clase/{id}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

#Configuracion
<!-- START_1becf1f76db2e30c1c20e7381c95a324 -->
## Configuracion: Store
Método para la creación de una instancia de Configuracion
params: [id_tema,id_gimnasio]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/configuracion/store" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/configuracion/store",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`POST api/configuracion/store`


<!-- END_1becf1f76db2e30c1c20e7381c95a324 -->

<!-- START_7ca6646ad0ee70bb3bf0c2e75ccaab33 -->
## Configuracion: Update
Método para la actualización de una instancia de Configuracion
params: [id,id_tema]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/configuracion/update" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/configuracion/update",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

## Configuracion: Destroy
Método para eliminar una instancia de Configuracion
params id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X DELETE "http://localhost/api/configuracion/destroy/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/configuracion/destroy/{id}",
    "method": "DELETE",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`DELETE api/configuracion/destroy/{id}`

## Configuracion: Index
Método para mostrar una lista de Configuracion
params: [page]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/configuracion" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/configuracion",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

<!-- START_12756ac0cd4f36cf95913e2b21ca0d25 -->
## Configuracion: Show
Método para mostrar una instancia de Configuracion
params: id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/configuracion/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/configuracion/{id}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

<!-- START_d029622baa3ac7afa1b0157c1d4b7fb2 -->
## Contacto: Store
Método para la creación de una instancia de Contacto
params: [nombre_completo,telefono,correo,horario_atencion_inicio,horario_atencion_fin,url_facebook]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/contacto/store" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/contacto/store",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

### HTTP Request

## Direccion: Show
Método para mostrar una instancia de Direccion
params: id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/direccion/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/direccion/{id}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

### HTTP Request
`GET api/direccion/{id}`

`HEAD api/direccion/{id}`

#Ejecucion
<!-- START_90dfb4d696d1e5aa4089f87a46baad0b -->
## Ejecucion: Store
Método para la creación de una instancia de Ejecucion
params: [id_usuario,id_wod,id_sesion]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/ejecucion/store" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/ejecucion/store",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`POST api/ejecucion/store`


<!-- END_90dfb4d696d1e5aa4089f87a46baad0b -->

<!-- START_fe44290d85384ab719214af5c195133d -->
## Ejecucion: Update
Método para la actualización de una instancia de Ejecucion
params: [id,id_usuario,id_wod,id_sesion]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/ejecucion/update" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/ejecucion/update",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`POST api/ejecucion/update`


<!-- END_fe44290d85384ab719214af5c195133d -->

<!-- START_6d91091731eee860e0284e86497df2e5 -->
## Ejecucion: Destroy
Método para eliminar una instancia de Ejecucion
params id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X DELETE "http://localhost/api/ejecucion/destroy/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/ejecucion/destroy/{id}",
    "method": "DELETE",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`DELETE api/ejecucion/destroy/{id}`

## Ejecucion: Index
Método para mostrar una lista de Ejecucion
params: [page]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/ejecucion" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/ejecucion",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

## Ejecucion: Show
Método para mostrar una instancia de Ejecucion
params: id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/ejecucion/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/ejecucion/{id}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

#Ejercicio
<!-- START_8d2642953ebb3250f1982639f83fb31c -->
## Ejercicio: Store
Método para la creación de una instancia de Ejercicio
params: [nombre,descripcion,instrucciones,img,video,id_tipo_ejercicio]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/ejercicio/store" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/ejercicio/store",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`POST api/ejercicio/store`


<!-- END_8d2642953ebb3250f1982639f83fb31c -->

```javascript
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/ejercicio/destroy/{id}",
    "method": "DELETE",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

## Ejercicio: Index

params: [page, q, id_tipo_ejercicio]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/ejercicio" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/ejercicio",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

    console.log(response);
});
```

## Ejercicio: Show
Método para mostrar una instancia de Ejercicio
params: id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/ejercicio/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/ejercicio/{id}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

#Gimnasio
<!-- START_134581706ef9b4122dd48b9105c206bb -->
## Gimnasio: Store
Método para la creación de una instancia de Gimnasio
params: [nombre,logo,pagina,descripcion,puntos_por_asistencia,id_tema]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/gimnasio/store" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/gimnasio/store",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`POST api/gimnasio/store`

Método de búsqueda para gimnasios por nombre. El parámetro q es el texto a buscar.

params: [q]

> Example request:

```bash

-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript

    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/gimnasio/buscar",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

> Example response:

```json
{
    "message": "Unauthenticated."
}
```

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X DELETE "http://localhost/api/membresia/destroy/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/membresia/destroy/{id}",
    "method": "DELETE",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

### HTTP Request
`GET api/tema/{id}`

`HEAD api/tema/{id}`


<!-- END_77f7424ac1ae713855facc0a59b62955 -->

#User
<!-- START_3fe85d11bc564d9432f61e61d0e63293 -->
## User: Store
Método para la creación de una instancia de User
params: [email,nombre, password, apellido_paterno,apellido_materno,telefono,fecha_nacimiento,sexo,tipo_sangre,consumer_token,id_titulo,id_gimnasio,id_sucursal]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/user/store" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/user/store",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`POST api/user/store`


<!-- END_3fe85d11bc564d9432f61e61d0e63293 -->

<!-- START_52fd5e8ee8adce4b3e2673d52c022a6f -->
## User: Users by gym
params: [id_rol, id_gimnasio]
Método para mostrar a todos los usuarios de un gimnasio en específico

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/user/byGym" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/user/byGym",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

## User: Update
Método para la actualización de una instancia de User
params: params: [nombre,apellido_paterno,apellido_materno,telefono,fecha_nacimiento,sexo,tipo_sangre,consumer_token,id_titulo,id_gimnasio,id_sucursal]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/user/update" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/user/update",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

## User: Usuarios inhabilitados
params: []
Devuelve una lista de los usuarios inhabilitados en el servicio, para la pantalla de activar usuarios

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/user/usuarios-inhabilitados" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/user/usuarios-inhabilitados",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

## User: Habilitar Usuario
params: [id_usuario]
Permite regresar a un usuario del cementerio al campo de batalla.

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/user/habilitar-usuario" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/user/habilitar-usuario",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

### HTTP Request
`GET api/user`

`HEAD api/user`


<!-- END_2ea88ff35aa222f5582e50f39a2b35fd -->

<!-- START_8ff0f42739fc7113fcacca8ef86d1ce2 -->
## User: Show
Método para mostrar una instancia de User
params: id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/user/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/user/{id}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

### HTTP Request
`GET api/sucursal/entrenadores/{id_sucursal}`

`HEAD api/sucursal/entrenadores/{id_sucursal}`


<!-- END_bdd9772ca3170af0df5b5bab5c9345a1 -->

<!-- START_6e76ea3d37426f6cdd44518bdd036777 -->
## Sucursal: Destroy
Método para eliminar una instancia de Sucursal
params id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X DELETE "http://localhost/api/sucursal/destroy/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/sucursal/destroy/{id}",
    "method": "DELETE",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`DELETE api/sucursal/destroy/{id}`


<!-- END_6e76ea3d37426f6cdd44518bdd036777 -->

<!-- START_1c6d3aece79eacd4e905184b1be7ca6f -->
## Sucursal: Index
Método para mostrar una lista de Sucursal
params: [page]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/sucursal" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/sucursal",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

<!-- START_79280fbb8732822c3fd8b1739baee895 -->
## Sucursal: Show
Método para mostrar una instancia de Sucursal
params: id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/sucursal/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/sucursal/{id}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

### HTTP Request
`GET api/sucursal/{id}`

`HEAD api/sucursal/{id}`


<!-- END_79280fbb8732822c3fd8b1739baee895 -->

<!-- START_920d3f93a8d50842a9413cb804b33d6e -->
## Sucursal: Index by Gimnasio
params: [id_gimnasio]
Método que devuelve las sucursales a partir del id de un gimnasio

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/sucursal/bygym/{id_gimnasio}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/sucursal/bygym/{id_gimnasio}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

## TipoWod: Index
Método para mostrar una lista de TipoWod
params: [page]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/tipowod" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/tipowod",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

## Wod: Store
Método para la creación de una instancia de Wod
params: [id_tipo_wod,id_usuario,nombre,descripcion, rondas]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/wod/store" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/wod/store",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`POST api/wod/store`


<!-- END_76415c27916e21b84c4744a6ad3eb6cf -->

## Wod: Filtro
Filtra los Wods por nombre y tipo
params: [id_tipo_wod, nombre]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/wod/filtro" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/wod/filtro",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

## Wod: Destroy
Método para eliminar una instancia de Wod
params id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X DELETE "http://localhost/api/wod/destroy/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/wod/destroy/{id}",
    "method": "DELETE",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`DELETE api/wod/destroy/{id}`


<!-- END_449103547a69683a8da344b8e350f710 -->

<!-- START_f3e0429006ba4dda22a512f521744c10 -->
## Wod: Index
Método para mostrar una lista de Wod
params: [page]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/wod" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/wod",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

## Wod: Show
Método para mostrar una instancia de Wod
params: id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/wod/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/wod/{id}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

## Sesion: Store
Método para la creación de una instancia de Sesion
params: [id_profesor,id_clase,fecha_inicio,fecha_fin,id_sucursal,id_wod,notas_especiales,cupo]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/sesion/store" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/sesion/store",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`POST api/sesion/store`


<!-- END_2c684e3f1aa402ee27d62f55ed8795eb -->

<!-- START_2015da0de7763112c3b5586a93a17471 -->
## Sesion: Update
Método para la actualización de una instancia de Sesion
params: [id_profesor,id_clase,fecha_inicio,fecha_fin,id_sucursal,id_wod,notas_especiales,cupo]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/sesion/update" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/sesion/update",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`POST api/sesion/update`


<!-- END_2015da0de7763112c3b5586a93a17471 -->

<!-- START_107076d79b38ee3f64c825e0bfc3489c -->
## Sesion: Verificar
params: [id_sesion]
Permite ver si un usuario está registrado a una sesión. Devuelve data =&gt; true en
caso de existir relación y data =&gt; false de lo contrario.

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/sesion/usuario-suscrito" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/sesion/usuario-suscrito",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`POST api/sesion/usuario-suscrito`


<!-- END_107076d79b38ee3f64c825e0bfc3489c -->

<!-- START_5833f7f4e89c20412ae02e969120468e -->
## Sesión: Próximas sesiones
Devuelve una lista de las sesiones próximas en las que está inscrito el usuario.

params: []
*El usuario lo obtiene mediante el token de autenticación

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/sesion/proximas-sesiones" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/sesion/proximas-sesiones",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`POST api/sesion/proximas-sesiones`


<!-- END_5833f7f4e89c20412ae02e969120468e -->

<!-- START_73c91a9c4d377e2628b7e5a37766bbed -->
## Sesión: Por día y clase
Devuelve una lista de sesiones de acuerdo al día seleccionado y ordenados por clase.

params: [fecha]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/sesion/por-dia-y-clase" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/sesion/por-dia-y-clase",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

### HTTP Request
`GET api/sesion/por-dia-y-clase`

`HEAD api/sesion/por-dia-y-clase`


<!-- END_73c91a9c4d377e2628b7e5a37766bbed -->

<!-- START_3e985f3c078b78f8058131fb02fbacbf -->
## Sesion: Destroy
Método para eliminar una instancia de Sesion
params id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X DELETE "http://localhost/api/sesion/destroy/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/sesion/destroy/{id}",
    "method": "DELETE",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`DELETE api/sesion/destroy/{id}`


<!-- END_3e985f3c078b78f8058131fb02fbacbf -->

<!-- START_4f578b79edb1e2548dcf2cdc3fb0ebab -->
## Sesion: Index
Método para mostrar una lista de Sesion
params: [page]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/sesion" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/sesion",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

### HTTP Request

<!-- START_048975be749069a3006cc01d551b0c47 -->
## Sesion: Show
Método para mostrar una instancia de Sesion
params: id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/sesion/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/sesion/{id}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

> Example response:

## PeriodoClase: Store
Método para la creación de una instancia de PeriodoClase
params: [id_clase,id_dia,hora_inicio,hora_fin,id_ronda,id_profesor]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/periodoclase/store" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/periodoclase/store",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`POST api/periodoclase/store`


<!-- END_f72320e3724c6533d14fac1fa886b4f0 -->

<!-- START_7b42ba6128ece3b36182cf46fef9aef5 -->

## PeriodoClase: Destroy
Método para eliminar una instancia de PeriodoClase
params id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X DELETE "http://localhost/api/periodoclase/destroy/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/periodoclase/destroy/{id}",
    "method": "DELETE",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

## PeriodoClase: Index
Método para mostrar una lista de PeriodoClase
params: [page]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/periodoclase" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/periodoclase",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

## PeriodoClase: Show
Método para mostrar una instancia de PeriodoClase
params: id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/periodoclase/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/periodoclase/{id}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

```javascript
    console.log(response);
```

### HTTP Request
`GET api/rol`

`HEAD api/rol`


<!-- END_3f7cdd876c3a0281e21c430294c5dcfd -->

<!-- START_3ab31a2b24e8e9cf46f5daca73b50849 -->
## Rol: Show
Método para mostrar una instancia de Rol
params: id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/rol/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/rol/{id}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

## TipoMembresia: Store
Método para la creación de una instancia de TipoMembresia
params: [nombre, id_sucursal]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/tipomembresia/store" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/tipomembresia/store",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`POST api/tipomembresia/store`


<!-- END_fc6868bc8746597243c7319ea95e97db -->

## TipoMembresia: Por sucursal
Método para devolver los tipos de membresía por su sucursal
params: /id_sucursal

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/tipomembresia/por-sucursal/{id_sucursal}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/tipomembresia/por-sucursal/{id_sucursal}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

## TipoMembresia: Update
Método para la actualización de una instancia de TipoMembresia
params: [id, nombre]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/tipomembresia/update" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/tipomembresia/update",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

```javascript
    "headers": {

    console.log(response);
```

```bash
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,

    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
```

## TipoMembresia: Show
Método para mostrar una instancia de TipoMembresia
params: id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/tipomembresia/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/tipomembresia/{id}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

## TipoEjercicio: Index
Método para mostrar una lista de TipoEjercicio
params: [page]

> Example request:

```bash

-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/tipoejercicio",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

### HTTP Request
`GET api/tipoejercicio`

`HEAD api/tipoejercicio`


<!-- END_933e0e6c682cc968febfed2229638661 -->

<!-- START_c5644c7284f94057484a0cbf61875dc2 -->
## TipoEjercicio: Show
Método para mostrar una instancia de TipoEjercicio
params: id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/tipoejercicio/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/tipoejercicio/{id}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

## TipoRonda: Index
Método para mostrar una lista de TipoRonda
params: [page]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/tiporonda" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/tiporonda",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

## Ronda: Store
Método para la creación de una instancia de Ronda
params: [id_tipo_ronda,id_wod,nombre,duracion,repeticiones]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/ronda/store" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/ronda/store",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

`POST api/ronda/store`

## Ronda: Filtro
Filtra las rondas por nombre y por tipo
params: [id_tipo_ronda, nombre]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/ronda/filtro" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/ronda/filtro",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

### HTTP Request
`GET api/ronda/filtro`

## Ronda: Destroy
Método para eliminar una instancia de Ronda
params id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X DELETE "http://localhost/api/ronda/destroy/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/ronda/destroy/{id}",
    "method": "DELETE",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`DELETE api/ronda/destroy/{id}`


<!-- END_84f8011832617d2fcb476ceb066b586b -->

<!-- START_13723ce1dca7e96ae1a1f05a9c28757f -->
## Ronda: Index
Método para mostrar una lista de Ronda
params: [page]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/ronda" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/ronda",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

<!-- START_8eb0662eb429210dfaa69581e2b5691a -->
## Ronda: Show
Método para mostrar una instancia de Ronda
params: id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/ronda/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/ronda/{id}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

> Example response:

```json
{

    "exception": "Symfony\\Component\\HttpKernel\\Exception\\HttpException",
```

## Openpay: Add Customer
Add customer to Openpay platform
params: []

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/openpay/add-customer" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/openpay/add-customer",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`POST api/openpay/add-customer`


<!-- END_7ed6cdcacc7093e85a1a465d4c3da1c3 -->

<!-- START_200bb30ff4cfa6654fd6cb1911c2adf1 -->
## Openpay: Delete Customer
Elimina a un cliente (ADMIN)
params: /id_usuario
Esta función permite eliminar a un cliente de la lista con su id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X DELETE "http://localhost/api/openpay/delete-customer/{id_usuario}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/openpay/delete-customer/{id_usuario}",
    "method": "DELETE",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`DELETE api/openpay/delete-customer/{id_usuario}`

```javascript
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }

});
```

### HTTP Request
`GET api/categoria/buscar`

`HEAD api/categoria/buscar`


<!-- END_fdda7edcf0dc8409f0985a8ac00f7a29 -->

<!-- START_ccd00572f2eda7f468491066473e0882 -->
## Categoria: Destroy
Método para eliminar una instancia de Categoria
params id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X DELETE "http://localhost/api/categoria/destroy/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/categoria/destroy/{id}",
    "method": "DELETE",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`DELETE api/categoria/destroy/{id}`


<!-- END_ccd00572f2eda7f468491066473e0882 -->

## Categoria: Index
Método para mostrar una lista de Categoria
params: [page]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/categoria" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/categoria",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

<!-- START_97df89569acdb53cc659afa735201442 -->
## Categoria: Show
Método para mostrar una instancia de Categoria
params: id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/categoria/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/categoria/{id}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

## Descuento: Store
Método para la creación de una instancia de Descuento
params: [id_articulo,id_tipo_descuento,id_tipo_aplicacion_descuento,descuento,cantidad_mayoreo]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/descuento/store" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/descuento/store",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`POST api/descuento/store`


<!-- END_5d4f64dcae1bc16296cd072966d709f9 -->

<!-- START_960a71bd1a3c3247bf8be6abf323d4ad -->
## Descuento: Update
Método para la actualización de una instancia de Descuento
params: [id_articulo,id_tipo_descuento,id_tipo_aplicacion_descuento,descuento,cantidad_mayoreo]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X PUT "http://localhost/api/descuento/update" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/descuento/update",
    "method": "PUT",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

## Descuento: Destroy
Método para eliminar una instancia de Descuento
params id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X DELETE "http://localhost/api/descuento/destroy/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/descuento/destroy/{id}",
    "method": "DELETE",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`DELETE api/descuento/destroy/{id}`

## Descuento: Index
Método para mostrar una lista de Descuento
params: [page]

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/descuento" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/descuento",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

### HTTP Request
`GET api/descuento`

`HEAD api/descuento`


<!-- END_e271e0c6e8e146367c7c11c7b63f847c -->

<!-- START_ad8c50fba4df7c11f50cf78b6fbcfab8 -->
## Descuento: Show
Método para mostrar una instancia de Descuento
params: id

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/descuento/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/descuento/{id}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```
